The wind calms, the roaring chaos goes silent. The Satetsu is numb to the sensations of thrill and excitement as the pot of rebellion begins to boil over.
  Yet.. there was a gnawing feeling in his chest that he needs to move.

<i><font color = white>&#34;..huh..?&#34;</font></i>
Something is off. There&#39;s malice approaching- No.. There&#39;s revenge drawing close. Who? Where?

Whatever it is, it&#39;s moving a lot faster than what Sogeki can actually keep up with- even with his trained visio.

   ..yet..

<font color = white>&#34;..found you,&#34;</font> He mutters under his breath as he bends at the knees. Chakra pours to the soles of his feet and without any hesitation he gets out of the way. He left behind nothing but a strand of hair- proof that he narrowly escaped disaster.

<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#5f5f5f>Satetsu, Sogeki descended gracefully towards the ground, the rush of air and the exhilaration of movement surrounding him. His keen senses and eagle-like eyesight allowed him to anticipate every detail, every motion around him, as if time slowed down. With precision honed through rigorous training, he prepared to land.

Just as he was about to touch down, an unexpected surge of chakra-infused chains wrapped around his limbs with startling force. His descent halted abruptly, twisting his body mid-air. Sogeki's eyes widened in surprise as he realized he was suddenly restrained, suspended in the air by unseen forces.

The chains held him firmly in place, suspending him above the ground. Sogeki's muscles tensed instinctively, his mind racing to comprehend the situation. Frustration and defiance welled up within him, yet he knew resisting now would only escalate the confrontation further.

Caught in the grip of the chakra chains, Sogeki's breaths came quick and controlled. He grappled with a mix of emotionsfrustration at being restrained, respect for the Commander's authority, and a burgeoning sense of understanding the consequences of his actions.</font></font></font>
